Municipal Health Bureau Arranges Free Cholera Vaccinations at Various Hospitals

Scheduled to Begin on the 15th of This Month

And Prepares to Expand Epidemic Prevention Publicity

According to predictions by numerous medical experts, this year is expected to be a year of epidemic prevalence. Therefore, the Municipal Health Bureau, in order to prevent cholera early and eradicate the epidemic, has specifically arranged, starting from the 15th of this month, to entrust 28 hospitals and clinics throughout the city to provide free vaccinations. They are also preparing to conduct expanded epidemic prevention publicity. Details are reported as follows:

Extensive Publicity

Since the cholera outbreak in Shanghai in 1932, the city's health authorities have worked hard to eradicate it, preventing the epidemic from spreading. This year marks the fourth anniversary. According to predictions by numerous experts, this year's epidemic is bound to be more serious than in previous years. Therefore, the Municipal Health Bureau, in order to ensure the safety of citizens' lives, is implementing preventive measures in advance, regularly convening meetings of various health agencies to discuss epidemic prevention, and preparing for city-wide expanded publicity to raise public awareness.

Free Vaccinations

The Municipal Health Bureau has issued a notice to all citizens regarding free cholera vaccinations, stating that in order to prevent cholera and protect the health of citizens, the bureau will begin providing free cholera vaccinations from the 15th of this month. In addition to organizing vaccination teams stationed at key locations to carry out vaccinations, it will also entrust various hospitals as vaccination sites to ensure widespread coverage. All citizens can go to the following locations for vaccinations. For groups of 30 or more people, the bureau can arrange for personnel to be sent for vaccinations at regular intervals. This is hereby announced.

Designated Hospitals

Designated hospitals and clinics for vaccinations: Fangxie Road, Shanghai South District Health Office; Jiangwan Health Office; Wusong Health Office; Gaoqiao Health Office; Zhabei Clinic, Minli Road, Zhabei; Xin Puyu Hall, Puyu West Road; Women and Children's Hospital, Fangxie Road; Waterside Pavilion Clinic, Xiaonanmen Street; Taizhou Hospital, Minguo Road, Xinqiao Street Intersection; Tongde Hospital, Tongfu Road; Shanghai Epidemic Hospital, Xizang Road; Huxi Commune, Laobosen Road; Lianyi West Hospital, Hanqiao Block; First Hospital of the Red Cross Society, Xinzha Road; Pingmin Charity Clinic, Dawangmiao Street; Nanyang Hospital, Xiaonanmen; Public Education Hall, Wenmiao Road; Labor Hospital, Xiaoshadu Road; Zhongde Hospital, Zhangjiabang, Jing'an Temple; First Aid Epidemic Hospital, North Xizang Road; Pudong Hospital, Lan Nidu, Pudong; Pushen Hospital, No. 1043 Xinmin Road; General Hospital of the Red Cross Society, Haige Road; Third Branch of the Red Cross Society, Waima Road, Shiliupu; Southeast Hospital, Hujun Camp; Children's Charity Clinic, Wuzhen Road; Hunan Public Maternity Hospital, Zhonghua Road, Danandou, totaling 28 locations.

Ministry of Industry Seeks Opinions on Establishing an Agricultural Capital Bureau

Deadline for Submission is the 15th of This Month

Various Banks in the City are Currently Studying the Proposal Separately

Minister of Industry Wu Dingchang convened a meeting of the financial community on the 2nd to discuss the establishment of the Agricultural Capital Bureau. It was decided that the capital would be divided into a fixed capital of 30 million yuan, allocated by the government; a working capital of 30 million yuan, to be borne by participating banks at 6 million yuan per year, payable in five years; and a revolving fund of an indefinite amount, to be supplied by participating banks through negotiation. After the organizational outline was approved, and in order to gather diverse perspectives, the Ministry is continuing to solicit opinions from various banks on the Agricultural Capital Bureau. These opinions must be submitted in writing to the Shanghai Banking Association by the 15th of this month, and the Association will then compile and forward them to the Ministry of Industry for reference. A second meeting is planned to be convened for detailed study, after which the capital will be paid in, and the Bureau is expected to be formally established on July 1st. The head office will be located in Nanjing, with branch offices established in important locations such as Shanghai, Hankou, and Tianjin. Commissioners will be stationed in various counties to handle all matters.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Cables Ministry of Industry Requesting Postponement of Animal Hide Inspection

Strict Attention Should be Paid During Hunting Season

Inspection Should Not be Implemented on Traded Finished Products

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Industry in Nanjing, stating that on the 2nd of this month, the City's Fur, Oil, and Bone Trade Association sent a letter stating that the Association had previously received from the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry the "Detailed Rules for the Implementation of Fur Inspection" and had been solicited for opinions. The Association believed that fur

Conditions are Unique

And its types are complex. Implementing inspection would encounter many obstacles. On October 7, 1935, the Association submitted a report outlining the difficulties to the Ministry, requesting exemption from implementation. Unexpectedly, on April 24, a letter was received from the Commodity Inspection Bureau stating, "This Bureau is preparing for fur inspection and convened a meeting at 10:00 AM on the 22nd of this month, inviting representatives of your Association, Lu [name] and Yuan [name], to attend. Mr. Lu and others requested consideration of the commercial situation and suggested that, except for large-volume exports of domestic rabbit skins, wild rabbit skins, lambskins, and [hide type] skins, inspection should be temporarily waived for other furs. As for inspection fees, it was agreed that domestic rabbits would be charged 10 cents per hundred skins, wild rabbit skins 5 cents per hundred skins, lambskins 1 cent per skin, and [hide type] skins 43 cents per metric ton. The decision was accepted and will be reported to the Ministry.

Scheduled Inspection

We hereby request you to take note. If your Association has any opinions on the grading standards for the inspection of the aforementioned skins in the previously sent draft of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of Fur Inspection, please inform us immediately for reference. This matter concerns inspection policy, and we hope your Association will assist in its implementation." This was deeply alarming. The Association had not received any notice from the Bureau to convene a meeting beforehand, nor had it designated any members as attending representatives. According to the two gentlemen themselves, they did not attend the meeting under official Association mandate, but merely attended the Bureau for discussions in their private capacities. The Association contacted Mr. Lu and Mr. Yuan separately to seek confirmation. The Association believes that it is currently outlining the difficulties of the Bureau's inspection and appealing for its suspension. However, the Bureau used the attendance of Mr. Lu and Mr. Yuan as

A Pretext for Attending the Meeting

If the Bureau held a formal meeting, why was no notice given beforehand? Furthermore, there were no records of the event. How can such a major event be confirmed without written documentation? Should representatives not have credentials to verify their full authority to attend? Such procedures are simple even in regular meetings, let alone in a decision made by inspection authorities concerning a professional association on a major event. This is something that the Association cannot accept. Furthermore, the promotion of inspection policy is a painstaking effort on the part of the authorities, and we dare not criticize it. However, examining the practices of various countries in the East and West, there are no regulations for the inspection of exported animal hides. Instead, they are tax-exempt to encourage export, as they are used to manufacture luxury decorative items. Therefore, exports are encouraged, and fundamental improvements are made to the materials themselves

To Increase Production

If rural producing areas regulate hunting seasons, compel hunters to register, and provide guidance, with severe penalties for those who hunt out of season or illegally, the materials can be gradually improved. Alternatively, rewards can be offered for raising and strictly protecting animals, and mechanical methods can be used for hunting to avoid injury, with the aim of gradually increasing production. Looking back at our country's hunters, they adhere to traditional methods, killing animals at any time, resulting in hidden scars and affecting their usefulness. Even after the start of spring in the lunar calendar, during the breeding season for animals, mothers and their offspring are harmed, leading to a gradual decline in production. During the years 1933-1934, exports of [hide type] skins, such as yellow weasels, reached over 3 million, but recently only exceeded 1 million. Exports of rubber skins reached 200,000-300,000, but recently did not reach 100,000. From this, it can be seen that various countries focus on fundamental remedies, so materials are good and production is abundant. Our country, on the other hand,

Inspects Goods That Have Already Been Traded

This is putting the cart before the horse and is bound to cause disputes between buyers and sellers. We fear that it will not achieve results but will instead cause harm. We do not believe that this was the initial intention of the Ministry of Industry to support hide merchants. The Association believes that if inspection is indeed implemented, it will be deeply painful and difficult to endure in silence. Therefore, we are reiterating our difficulties and humbly request that the Ministry consider the hardships of merchants and suspend the implementation of animal hide inspection. The Association received the letter at the meeting. Based on this, regarding the matter of animal hide inspection, the Association expressed dissent in a letter from the trade association on October 8 of last year. We telegraphed the Ministry, Commercial Word No. 38698, requesting the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau to investigate and respond before further notification. Now, according to the association's follow-up letter,

Improving Animal Hides

Should focus on strict attention during hunting season and should not be inspected when finished products are traded, as this would hinder the progress of trade. The statement is not without reason. Furthermore, when the Commodity Inspection Bureau convened a meeting to implement inspection, it did not formally invite the trade association to designate representatives to attend. Instead, it used Mr. Lu and Mr. Yuan from the industry as tools for making decisions, resulting in a decision that was not agreed to by the entire trade. The handling of the matter was also not properly done. We hereby report the situation and humbly request that the Ministry review and approve an order for the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau to postpone the implementation of animal hide inspection, to subtly inquire about the opinions of the entire trade, to carefully review the matter in the long term, to facilitate inspection policy, and to serve the public interest. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, respectfully.

Dockworkers' Leaders Welcome Qian Xueshi of the New Life Movement Corps Yesterday

There are over 100,000 dockworkers in Shanghai. Therefore, when Instructor Qian decided to come to Shanghai to inspect the New Life Movement, the leaders appointed Zhou Lilv, Guo Binghui, Liu Bin, Gao Yuancheng, and over 40 others as representatives to hold a welcome meeting at Mr. Zhou's residence in Xin Kaihe at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon and invited Instructor Qian to deliver a speech. Mr. Qian's topic was "How to Lead Dockworkers in Extraordinary Times." He first analyzed the quality and quantity of dockworkers, then described the responsibilities of dockworkers in extraordinary times and how to lead dockworkers in great detail. Instructor Qian's words were sincere, and the listeners were deeply moved.

Ren Lianchang of the New Village Construction Society Accused of Embezzlement

The China New Village Construction Society, located at No. 918 Edward Road, was founded by Zhang Yongnian from Cixi, who hired Ren Lianchang from Zhuji, Zhejiang, as the director of the business department. On August 1 of last year, Zhang went to the Dutch East Indies (Java) for business. When he returned to Shanghai on September 28, he discovered discrepancies in the accounts. He hired accountant Sun Zhongyao to audit the accounts. Accountant Sun found that Ren Lianchang had taken advantage of his position to embezzle public funds amounting to 3,593.88 yuan. After receiving the report, Zhang Yongnian reported the matter to the Chengdu Road Patrol, who dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. Zhang Yongnian then filed a public lawsuit against Ren Lianchang in the First Special Court, accusing him of embezzlement under Article 336 of the Criminal Law. The Special Court issued a summons for Ren Lianchang. However, after learning of the accusation, Ren Lianchang also hired a lawyer to file a countersuit against Zhang Yongnian in the criminal court of the First Special Court, accusing him of false accusation. The court has already held one hearing on the false accusation case. However, because there was a prior public lawsuit for embezzlement, the court ruled to temporarily suspend the trial of the false accusation case. Yesterday morning, Judge Tan Xinzhen took the bench in the Eighth Criminal Court to hear the public lawsuit for embezzlement. The defendant, Ren Lianchang, arrived with his defense attorney, Dai Jien, as summoned. Patrol lawyer Zhang Tianyin presented the case, stating that according to accountant Sun's report, it was discovered that the defendant had secretly used the funds submitted by the client Mei Hanqi, as well as the salary paid on behalf of Zhang Yongnian. Furthermore, the defendant paid for the repair of his personal car and the expenses of the "Commander's Office" from the construction society's accounts. In this way, the defendant embezzled a total of 3,593.88 yuan. After Judge Tan questioned the victim, Zhang Yongnian, and the defendant, Ren Lianchang, he ordered a new hearing to be held on the 11th of this month. The defendant, Ren Lianchang, was ordered to provide a surety of 3,600 yuan. Before the surety was provided, his defense attorney, Dai Jien, was allowed to be responsible for his release.

Heavy Fog in Shanghai Yesterday

Unable to Distinguish People a Few Steps Away

Import Vessels All Delayed

Heavy fog enveloped Shanghai yesterday morning, making it impossible to distinguish people a few steps away. As a result, vessels entering the port from the Yangtze River and the sea were delayed. The details are as follows:

Heavy Fog

The weather this spring has been unusually abnormal. Although it is almost the end of spring, the climate is still cold. For the past half month, there has been continuous rain. Yesterday, after dawn, heavy fog returned. Visibility was poor at a short distance. It was impossible to work indoors without turning on the lights. The fog gradually dissipated around 9 AM. Heavy rain returned at 5 PM in the afternoon.

Vessel Delays

Due to the heavy fog yesterday morning, vessels entering the port from the Yangtze River and the sea, such as the Shuang Hua, Hongda, Jiangda, British vessel Xinjiang, and Japanese vessel Ruiyang Maru, were all delayed. Arrival times were later than usual. The takeoff and arrival times of the China Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Hankou-Xi'an and Eastbound flights were also delayed.

Fine Reduced from 100,000 Yuan to 5,000 Yuan

The Haichang steamer of the Haichang Steamer Company, located at No. 15 Sijing Road, with a gross tonnage of 954 tons and a net tonnage of 523 tons, was leased to a Japanese merchant by the Dalian agency at the end of January of this year for a monthly rent of 5,000 yuan. Wing On Banking and Investment Company Creditors' Meeting: Chamber of Commerce Announces Postponement

Registration Still in Progress

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, in accordance with bankruptcy law, accepted the Wing On Banking and Investment Company's debt liquidation case. A creditors' meeting was convened at the Chamber of Commerce yesterday afternoon at 2 PM. Present were Chamber of Commerce representative Ke Ganchen, accountant Xu Yongzuo, debtor representative Zhang Henghai, and over eighty creditors. Chairman Ke Ganchen announced that the total debt of Wing On Banking and Investment Company was 225,303.9 yuan. Only over 65,000 yuan had been registered, accounting for just over one-third of the total debt. According to Article 27 of the Bankruptcy Law, a resolution for reconciliation at a creditors' meeting requires the consent of more than half of the creditors present, and the total amount they represent must account for more than three-quarters of the total unsecured debt. Therefore, as of today, the amount of debt registered has not reached the statutory amount and should be postponed. Registration will continue. The meeting was adjourned after the announcement.

Fresh Meat Industry to Adjust Prices

Scarce Supply Leads to High Pork Prices

The Shanghai pork industry, due to the recent scarcity of fresh pork and high pork prices, is finding it difficult to operate. It is reported that a meeting of industry members will be convened to discuss solutions. According to insiders, the reasons for the recent scarcity of fresh pork supply from various regions are: 1. Rural bankruptcy in northern Jiangsu last year and low commodity prices, making the sideline of raising pigs unprofitable for rural areas. 2. This year's high grain prices have made pig feed expensive. 3. Farmers in northern Jiangsu are unwilling to engage in sideline businesses, and the number of households raising fresh pigs is decreasing daily, resulting in a sharp drop in supply to Shanghai, nearly 40%. Due to the relationship between less supply and more demand, pork prices are rising daily, with no hope of falling. The selling price of meat must be adjusted.

Following the robbery of the Lixin small steamer of the Shenhu Lixing Inland Waterway Shipping Bureau, the industry association immediately sent a telegram to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs requesting protection. The text of the telegram is as follows: Zhenjiang, Director Yu Jun of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs. Respectfully submitted, Lixing Shipping Bureau's Lixin small steamer, a member of the association, was robbed on April 27 while sailing from Shanghai to Huzhou. At 10 PM that night, in the Yecheng Temple area of Malan Port, it was suddenly stopped by twelve bandits, all speaking with a northern Jiangsu accent, who fired their guns. All crew and passengers had their legal tender searched and robbed, totaling over 800 yuan. In addition to reporting the case to the Pingwang Public Security Bureau for investigation, the association believes that the best way to protect the Shenhu passenger vessels is to follow the Jiangsu Province's Inland Waterway Shipping Inspection and Apprehension Measures, dispatching patrol boats from the First District of the Water Police to escort the vessels between Minhang and Pingwang. We previously sent a telegram to you requesting approval for implementation. We received approval order Xuanzi No. 350 on April 17, 1936, stating that it would be difficult to dispatch boats to escort all the frequent upstream and downstream voyages, and instructing the heads of the First and Second Districts of the Water Police to provide careful protection. Unexpectedly, protection has not been effective, and another robbery has occurred. In this situation, not only is it difficult for shipping merchants to operate, but it also hinders public security on the water. As farming season begins, farmers will be returning to their hometowns to cultivate the land, and passenger vessels will be more crowded. If bandits are allowed to run rampant, farmers will regard the ships as dangerous, affecting the rural economy, which is a great concern. The association witnesses the dangerous situation and can no longer remain silent. We dare to reiterate our previous request, respectfully requesting you to order the First District of the Water Police to assign two patrol boats to escort the vessels, which is essential for effectiveness, so that transportation will not be hindered. The telegram is urgent and awaits your orders. Chairman Han Yimin of the Shanghai Inland Waterway Shipping Industry Association.

Original Trial Sentenced to Life Imprisonment

Lawyer Luo Zhaoxin was assassinated on Zhejiang Road in Qinghe Lane a few years ago. His son, Luo Yusheng, 22 years old, was the director of education at Mingchen Elementary School on Xinqiao Road in Nanshi. Suspecting that the murder of his father was related to Jin Daishi, a woman from Jinhua living at No. 459 Be河南路, he gathered a group of people and went to her residence at 8:30 AM on September 23 of last year, carrying axes, and killed both Jin Daishi and her maid, Luo Guo. He stole valuables and fled. Later, Huishi police detective Shang Wu arrested Luo Yusheng and sent him to the First Special Court for interrogation. He was found guilty of joint murder and sentenced to life imprisonment, and one year for theft, to be served concurrently with life imprisonment, and deprived of his civil rights for life. The defendant, Luo Yusheng, was dissatisfied with the sentence and appealed. The police also believed that Luo had committed robbery and murder, and that life imprisonment was not sufficient to cover his guilt. The Legal Department lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, presented the reasons and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court. Judge Yu repeatedly opened hearings and conducted detailed inquiries and declared the case closed. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yu Hua, along with Judges Zhong and Wang, announced the verdict: The original judgment is revoked. Luo Yusheng is sentenced to death for joint robbery and murder, deprived of his civil rights for life, and the two axes used in the crime are confiscated. Luo Yusheng's appeal is rejected.

Blessing Home for the Incurably Ill New Church Completed

Mr. Lu Bohong, a leader in the local Catholic community and a philanthropist, founded the Puzi Sanatorium last year in Beiqiao, specializing in the treatment of mental illness, neurological disorders, and various types of madness. He hired expert doctors and nurses for diagnosis and care. There are currently over 200 patients in the hospital. He has cured many cases of chronic diseases that have been untreatable for many years. In order to facilitate prayers for the male and female doctors, nurses, and Catholic patients in the community, Mr. Lu built a new church within the sanatorium. The church's style adopts a medieval Roman design, resplendent and magnificent, like the current St. Paul's Basilica in Rome. The interior is exquisite and magnificent, with ample light. In the center is an image of Our Lady of Perpetual Help, enshrined as the patron saint, implying a plea to Our Lady to show great mercy and grant all patients an early recovery. At 8 AM yesterday morning, Bishop Hui of the Shanghai Diocese was invited to perform the blessing and pray for peace. The high Mass was celebrated with full honors by the parish priest Zhang of Dongjiadu Catholic Church, representing Liu Lijiashi. Lu Bohong and Zhu Zhiyao were liturgical ministers. Lu Yin Geng and his brothers, all members of the Catholic Action Association, as well as representatives from various districts, such as Xu Zongze, editor of the Sacred Doctrine Magazine, leaders and priests of various associations, Song Hanzhang, General Manager of the Bank of China, Wang Baolun, Director of the Central Bank, He Lizhong, Gu Shouxi, and local and foreign Catholics, men and women, numbering no less than 2,000, gathered together. The ceremony was grand and solemn. The Zhenxiu Middle School Orchestra and Choir were responsible for the music and singing during the Mass. The sound was loud and resonant, the music harmonious and melodious. The hall was filled with fragrant fresh flowers and bright electric lights. The ceremony lasted for three hours before concluding. After a group photo was taken in front of the church, refreshments were served, and the various departments were visited, all expressing satisfaction before dispersing.

Ning County Government Replies to Ningbo Association Telegram

Suspension of Relocation of Graves in the Old City Area

The Ningbo Association in Shanghai, concerned about the excavation and relocation of graves in various towns and townships of Ningbo, which has aroused strong indignation among the public, convened an emergency meeting of its executive and supervisory committee on the 2nd of this month, resolving to send telegrams to the central government requesting rectification and to organize a special committee to handle all aspects of the case. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that the association, because the excavation of graves in various towns and townships has not stopped, sent a telegram to the Ning County government ordering a strict halt to the activity. The telegram from the association to County Magistrate Chen of Ning County is recorded below: Ning County Magistrate Chen Xunjian, Ningbo grave case, our association has repeatedly submitted reports to the provincial government and received approval. We hear that the Department of Civil Affairs is preparing detailed measures and will promulgate them soon. Before the measures are received, please strictly order all towns and townships in the city and countryside not to rashly excavate any more graves. Ningbo Association in Shanghai, Yu Hede, etc. The reply telegram from the County Magistrate is copied below: Shanghai Ningbo Association, The telegram has been received. The county's grave removal is being carefully planned in accordance with orders. The order to demolish and relocate within the city limits has been suspended. Please acknowledge. County Magistrate Chen Dong of Ning County.

Another Appeal from Tea Merchants in Anhui

Cao Yunjie Represents Petition to Reduce Tax Rates

The Tea Industry Associations of the counties of Xiuning, Yixian, Qimen in Anhui Province, nominated Mr. Cao Lingjie, former Chairman of the Southern Anhui Tea Appraisal Committee, as their representative to petition Beijing and Anhui to reduce tax rates this year. The short-term tea sales tax in Anhui Province, since the promulgation of the Business Tax Regulations in 1931, stipulates a tax of 0.5% on exported tea and 1% on tea sold domestically. In 1935, regardless of export or domestic sales, the tax was 1% with an additional 1.5% for the Security Team, totaling 1.2 yuan per dan. The Security Team expenses have always been added to the land tax, so tea farmers and tea merchants both bear the burden. Now, an additional tax is levied on boxed tea, which is unavoidable duplication. At a time when rural areas are bankrupt and Chinese tea is declining, tea farmers and tea merchants are in a precarious situation. Therefore, Mr. Cao was specially nominated to petition Beijing and Anhui in order to reduce tax rates and alleviate business difficulties. It is reported that the representative has arrived in Beijing and may soon be transferred to Anhui.

Shanghai Streetlights: Yapu Er Factory Continues to Supply

Since 1931, all of the city's streetlights have been purchased by the Municipal Bureau of Public Works from the China Yapu Er Electric Appliance Factory. In each subsequent tender, because the Yapu Er products are inexpensive and of good quality, the factory has been the supplier for the past six years. This year, the Bureau of Public Works collected various light bulbs on the market and had experts conduct precise tests on them. A public tender was also advertised, which attracted a great deal of interest. The results were announced publicly on the 23rd of last month, and the Yapu Er Factory won the bid again. It is reported that the factory received formal notification from the Municipal Bureau of Public Works yesterday to continue supplying the city's streetlights.

Observation of the Life of the Chinese Nation

— Liu Xiang, Deputy Head of the New Movement Inspection Group

The composition of a nation, from a social point of view, is of course nothing more than two aspects: nature and culture. Nature is the objective environment, and culture is the subjective force. Because a nation needs to adapt to its objective environment, its subjective force has to evolve with the objective. Ancient humans were in the stage of "man competing with beasts," so their culture was the era of stone tools and pottery. Modern humans are in the stage of "man competing with nature," so their culture is the era of science and chemistry. Modern humans, in addition to "man competing with nature," have added the trend of "man competing with man," so their culture, in addition to science and chemistry, must also add political and economic issues. This proves whether the existence and growth of a nation. His culture should adapt to their environment, and at the same time, their environment will be further developed through their culture. The so-called "theory of evolution," the so-called "survival competition," and the so-called population problem, all of which are, in short, to study whether a nation is progressing or declining in the current stage?

To study whether a nation's culture is suitable for the objective environment, whether it is expressed from the culture or reflected from the objective, the life of the nation is the focus of this issue.

The Chinese nation has gone through more than 4,000 years of evolution, sometimes prosperous and sometimes declining. Now it has reached the most cutting-edge era. From the perspective of the foreign environment, the increase in the population of the great powers and imperialists, the development of culture, and the rapid advancement of the economy, the first place in the quantity and quality of the Chinese nation has long been shaken and collapsed! From the perspective of the internal situation, rural bankruptcy, natural disasters and bandits, the crisis of the nation is more deeply latent. Here, it seems that the more difficult the objective environment in China is, the more difficult it is for the Chinese nation to adapt to life. In recent years, pessimists who complain about the sky and blame others, romantics who are decadent and disappointed, and people who betray the nation and lose their conscience are everywhere. In fact, everyone has forgotten that objective misfortune comes from the fact that their own lives cannot adapt to the times. They are reversing the cause and effect, and always only expect good luck to come. Waiting for the rabbit is more than just losing the rabbit. India is dead, and the Jews are dead. If the Chinese nation does not save itself, why can't it die!

Before we want to innovate a nation's life, the prior understanding must be dissected from the vertical and horizontal aspects of this nation, and then we can understand the crux of the problem and correct and guide it!

From the Zhou and Qin Dynasties to the present, there have been about four major divisions in the life history of the Chinese nation. In each division, the life of this nation has undergone a drastic change, adapting their lives from the old stage to another new stage.

The first division was the Zhou and Qin Dynasties. At that time, the Han people were breeding in the Yellow River Basin. There were barbarians outside and natural disasters inside. How did our nation grow in struggle? At least at that time, the life of the nation was martial, supported the leader, worked hard for production, and admired morality. The so-called "I am the king of my land, and my conquest is meritorious!" and "Cultivate at its time, and the people will enjoy it!" "Teach with its way, and the people will be righteous!" This can prove the life of that time. By the time of the Warring States Period, the lives of ordinary people gradually became selfish and self-interested, and followed the path of romantic consumption. The so-called "If the upper and lower levels compete for profit, the country is in danger!" "There are fat horses in the stables, and there are starving people in the fields!" So it ended up dying in Qin, and Qin ended up being trapped by the Hu!

The second division was from the Han Dynasty to the Six Dynasties. In this division, the Chinese nation has progressed towards the Yangtze River Basin. At that time, the life of the nation can be divided into three paragraphs: the martial arts of the Han Dynasty, the culture of the Han Dynasty, and the politics of the Han Dynasty, which proved the fact that this nation had a drastic outward development, and their lives were honest, serious, and productive. The so-called "civilians have no fur without banquets," "every family with ten rooms must have stored grain," and the most things about integrity were also in the Han Dynasty, such as Xia Shi Shu Jiang, Su Wu's unyielding, and Ti Ying saving her father. It can be seen how the national spirit was at that time. This is the first stage. Let's see what the life of the nation was like in the Jin Dynasty? The customs of ordinary people were exaggerated, unproductive, and undisciplined. The upper class talked about Qing, and the lower class were leisurely. Moreover, "Wushisan," a drug like opium, was the most popular hobby at that time. Therefore, the Western Jin Dynasty perished, the Eastern Jin Dynasty split, the Eight Kings rebelled, and the Five Hus were in chaos. At the end of the Jin Dynasty, the Chinese nation had no peace! This is the second stage. Let's look further down, what was the life of our nation like in the Northern and Southern Dynasties? Romantic decadence, romantic extravagance, the relics of Jinling rouge powder, and the enjoyment of the scholar-officials of Jiangnan, the decline of the Chinese nation can be said to have reached its extreme in that era! This is the third stage in this division.

The third division was from the Sui and Tang Dynasties to the Northern and Southern Song Dynasties. In this division, the life of the nation can be divided into two stages: The first stage was the Tang Dynasty, the revival of the Han people. From the political achievements of that time, such as Taizong's cultural rule, the Ming Dynasty's revision, the conquest of the Turks, the subjugation of the Tibetans, the communication of Korea, and the entry into Nanyang, how was the Chinese nation breeding? Their lives were firm, arduous, upward, and trained. The "Tun Jun" system at that time can be said to be the current military training, and the "Ke Nong" system at that time can be said to be the predecessor of the current rural revival. The people of the Tang Dynasty were also through hardships and lived clean and simple lives, although there were weaknesses in the middle of the remnants of the Tang Dynasty and the Anshi Rebellion! The second stage was the declining Song Dynasty. As soon as we see history, we will remember the Song Dynasty nation. It was oppressed by the Liao, Jin, and Mongolian throughout its years. Indeed, what was the life of the nation like at that time? Buddhist and Taoist ideas were very popular. Scholar-officials only talked about reason and forgot about military preparations. Civilians only knew how to love peace and live in peace, but they did not know how to cheer up. The Northern Song Dynasty perished, and the Southern Song Dynasty was in Jiangnan. The life of the court and the public at that time was whitewashing peace. Taking the past as a lesson for the present, how different is it! Therefore, it was trapped in Liao, succumbed to Jin, and eventually perished in Yuan.

The fourth division was the era in which the Chinese nation lost the country twice, from Yuan to Ming to Qing. However, in this division, we can see the great power of the Chinese nation, based on the Han people, to promote their assimilation. Incorporating the spirit of "Jurchen" and "Timur" into the decadent life of the Han people at that time, the history of the life of the Chinese nation changed again. The famous "Yellow Peril" in world history, and the unprecedented expansion of the Chinese territory, to this day, the national hero Genghis Khan is still praised by the people. The life of the Chinese nation at that time can be said to be the entire militarization, the so-called life of ancient chariots and iron cavalry. Although the Ming Dynasty was very weak in national military power, the economic prosperity of the Chinese nation was achieved by the Ming Dynasty to some extent. Sanbao eunuch, the only navigator in China, first went to Nanyang by sea, and at that time, the life of the nation still retained a little of the spirit of outward development left over from the Yuan Dynasty. By the time of the Qing Dynasty, this was a drastic change in the Chinese nation. How heroic was the first half of the Qing Dynasty, and how diligent and frugal was the life of the people. However, since the second half of the Qing Dynasty, the corruption of China's internal affairs and the failure of diplomacy have shown the darkness and turmoil of the life of this nation everywhere. There is no vitality at all. Just seeing the popularity of opium can summarize everything at that time!

Of course, before examining the life of the current stage, from historical observations, we can summarize and judge. The rise and fall of the Chinese nation is completely related to how they live. If their lives can be invigorated, no matter how complex and difficult the objective environment is, in fact, they can also adapt and develop. Please see what kind of situation is the environment and life of our nation today?

At present, the international environment is watching China surrounded in two different ways. The first is with the market as the goal, attempting the redistribution of the world. Abyssinia has been merged into Italy, the seriousness of the German-Austrian issue, the waves of the Suez Canal, the tension of the Strait of Gibraltar, and the black shadows in the West are accelerating the crisis in the Far East and China. The Chinese nation is located inside the two major powers of Japan and Russia. Whether it is the redization of Asia or the Monroe Asia, this nation has no possibility of gaining a foothold. The second is surrounded by the Chinese nation under the public example of survival of the fittest according to the law of natural survival. The stagnation of China's population, the abandonment of China's reserves, the weakness of national military power, and the corruption of national life are all counter-evidences to the prosperity of other ethnic groups such as the English, Latin, Caucasian, Taihe, and Teutonic, the progress of science, the expansion of military preparations, the increase in population, the insufficient land, the exhaustion of raw materials, the unevenness of colonies, and the various needs of living conditions. It is impossible to solve their internal contradictions without starting to invade the weak, and the old Chinese nation is bearing the brunt! However, looking back at the Chinese nation, how will it rise to adapt and fight against this complex and difficult environment in the future? Not only is there no such preparation and training, but it is still falling more deeply. We can see the reasons for the past demise in history, which is really chilling!

Of course, we now need to ask, how should our nation's life adapt to this complex environment? Here are only three paths for us to strive for: The first is to use the life of national self-defense to deal with the complex international environment. Although the world in 1936 is an era when weak nations are bullied everywhere, it is also a period of great alliances between weak nations that constitute a line of resistance. As long as we see Egypt, the recent anti-British movement of the Arab nation, Turkey's armed Dardanelles and Bosporus Straits, the power of the Spanish People's Front, and the mobilization of the Austrian border troops, no weak nation is not working hard for their self-defense. In such an international environment, the only thorough means for the Chinese nation is to rise up and defend our country! Because we want to defend ourselves, life must be militarized. Organize ourselves, train ourselves, discipline is the spirit of our lives, and machinery is the order of our lives. In peacetime, we are members of the nation, and in wartime, we are all soldiers of the nation. Secondly, we must use the life of national self-sufficiency to deal with the environment of international economic panic. The current stage of China's national economy is not uneven distribution, but no production. The way out for China's economy is not to invade others, but to live independently of its own nation and not rely on others. The only problem is to become productive. In recent years, in the international economic situation, the Soviet Union's abandonment of the economic policy of socialism with machines, the large-scale control methods of the United States, the colonial barriers of Britain, the concentration of gold in France, and the new national debt agreement in Germany are all efforts to do the work of raising, in order to cope with the extraordinary situation. Of course, China is no exception. It seems that China's work of raising today is more important than others. The so-called war has no surplus grain, and the room is empty. Although we are determined to do it, it is not allowed in fact. Therefore, because of the sake of raising, the national life needs to be simple and plain, save consumption, work hard for production, pay attention to various collective savings in peacetime, increase labor, and control the raw materials of materials and limit the waste of each individual in wartime, in the poor environment in all aspects, we have laid a foundation. The third is to use the life of national self-love to maintain this decadent and loose national consciousness, in order to cope with the current sharp international era. Looking around, the recent revival of heroism in the German nation, the right-wing trend of the Teutonic national thought in Europe, the strictness of the Slavic national red organization, and the advocacy of the Asian lifeline of the Yamato nation are all drumming up the tension of the national spirit to solve the difficulties of each individual. The shaking of national consciousness in China in recent years, and the tendency of "everyone can be a monarch," has created a large number of traitors who betray the nation. Therefore, the life of our nation must be artistic, and we must do the task of teaching. Ten years of teaching and gathering, one battle and dominance, "this is the lesson in history. Our current life, at a minimum, must achieve a healthy, rational, scientific, and conscientious life that is useful. It is not an empty and mysterious cultivation, but a practical morality that touches the heart and responds to things. It can also be said that it establishes the elements of survival from the instinct of human nature.

Indeed, the life we are trying to innovate is nothing more than these three points: teaching to establish oneself, raising to relieve poverty, and defending to resist insults. The three are equal in time, linked, and unified. Assuming that our national life has really reached this stage, no matter how complex the objective environment is, we can adapt to it. "The fittest survive," and the revival of our nation is, in fact, not difficult to count the days and wait.

Special Issue on the Completion of the New Clubhouse of the China Aviation Association

Overview of the Construction of the New Clubhouse of the China Aviation Association

In order to lay the foundation for the China Aviation Association to save the country through aviation and develop the cause of civil aviation, the fourth meeting of the Board of Directors decided on January 15, 1935, to build a clubhouse and an exhibition hall. The 25th meeting of the Standing Committee of the Board of Directors on February 25 also appointed four directors, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Yao Xijiu, and Li Dachao, to be responsible for the planning. Architect Dong Dayou was commissioned to design the building. The Shanghai Municipal Government allocated ten acres of land south of the museum in the city center, bordering the Qiu River to the south, and Fushou Zuo Road and Fu Nan Zuo Road to the east and west. The construction plan was repeatedly revised and decided. The style adopted was aircraft type, the exterior was decorated with artificial stone, and the medium and shallow carvings were simple and majestic. The bottom floor of the nose is the reception room, the upper floors of the wings are the aviation library and the exhibition hall, the bottom floor of the wings is also the aviation exhibition hall, the bottom floor of the fuselage and tail is the office, the upper floor of the nose is the memorial hall, the upper floor of the fuselage is the auditorium, and the upper floor of the tail is also the office. It is three stories high, with a handrail leaning against the wall and spiraling upwards, forming a circle in the middle. Looking up from the ground, you can see the blue sky and white sun glass on the top floor, which is dazzling. The circular wall on the highest floor is inlaid with marble name steles, engraved with the names of members, to be passed down forever. It was contracted by Jiutai Jinji Construction Factory, started on July 19, and held a foundation laying ceremony on October 12. It was originally scheduled to be completed by the end of December, but due to the loose foundation, the memorial hall roof could not be built and renovated on the same day, and it was completed on March 20 of this year, which lasted ten months.

The sanitary heating equipment was contracted by Langji Engineering Firm. Each room is equipped with a water radiator. The electric wires and lamps are contracted by Dahua Hydropower Company and Yuanfeng Architectural Decoration Company respectively. The wood is made of Liu'an wood, and the style is novel and simple, and is contracted by Shuimingchang Wood Company. The garden landscape is arranged by Shanghai Plantation. The total project and equipment cost 114,711.29 yuan in national currency.

The above is the construction process of the new clubhouse of the association. Today's completion ceremony will be reported simply.

General Overview of the Chinese Aviation Association's Affairs

(A) Formation of the Association

Since the September 18th Incident, the people of the nation have felt the weakness of our country's air defense. Requests to the government to expand the air force and petitions to organize aviation patriotic societies have been made one after another. The central government immediately instructed the Ministry of Military Affairs to send personnel to Shanghai to liaise with leaders from all walks of life to prepare for the organization. It wasn't until November of the 21st year of the Republic of China that the Ministry of Military Affairs forwarded to the National Government a list of twenty-one people, including Wang Xiaolai and Shi Liangcai, to be appointed as directors. Thus, the Aviation Patriotic Society was officially established. Subsequently, the central government, recognizing that the aviation patriotic movement required the concerted efforts of the government and the people, especially emphasizing unified methods and comprehensive planning, should be sustainable and effective, entrusted Mayor Wu Tiecheng to consult with the directors of the Aviation Patriotic Society on expanding the organization and renaming it the Chinese Aviation Association. It was established on New Year's Day of the 20th year of the Republic of China. On that day, representatives of the National Government, Mr. Wu Tiecheng, and representatives of the Executive Yuan, Mr. Chu Minyi, delivered earnest speeches. The guests who attended the ceremony were also enthusiastic. It was a grand and unprecedented occasion. Governments and military and political circles, and leaders in Nanjing, Beiping, Guihua, Jinan, Kaifeng, Zhangjiakou, Gunzhou, Xi'an, Huoshan, Shaanxi, Anhui, Ningxia, and other places sent congratulatory telegrams to the meeting, demonstrating that the aviation patriotic movement was a matter of concern for the entire nation.

Attached: List of Directors: Wang Xiaolai, Wang Zhengting, Wang Zhiyuan, Shi Liangcai, Zhu Qinglan, Du Yuesheng, Lin Kanghou, Lin Wojiang, Li Fusun, Hu Wenhu, Hu Yunzhuang, Chen Guangfu, Huang Bingheng, Zhang Huichang, Zhang Gongquan, Weng Zhaoyuan, Zhang Boling, Yu Qiaqing, Liu Peiquan, Xiong Xiling, Dai Kuisheng.

(B) Progress of the Association's Affairs

After the establishment of the Association in January of the 20th year of the Republic of China, in the first two years, the affairs of the Association were still in the planning and promotion stages, with little to report. Towards the end of the second year, after an internal reorganization, the affairs of the Association became increasingly complex. Here is a summary of the work done:

Improving the Overall Organization: The Association originally had twenty-one directors, who mutually elected one managing director and appointed one secretary-general, who, under the direction of the managing director, handled all daily affairs. Since the establishment of the Association, the managing director, Lin Wojiang, concurrently served as secretary-general. In September of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, Mr. Lin resigned from his concurrent position as secretary-general due to illness. After deliberation by the standing committee, Yao Xijiu was appointed as acting secretary-general. Subsequently, at the end of October, at a board meeting, Director Wu Tiecheng proposed "improving the organization of the Association," "recruiting specialized talent," and "actively developing the Association's affairs," and the following matters were resolved: 1. Director Weng Zhaoyuan's whereabouts have been unknown since the establishment of the Association, and the government is requested to appoint Mr. Kong Xiangxi as a director of the Association. 2. Add two managing directors, with Directors Wu Tiecheng and Kong Xiangxi appointed to these positions. 3. Managing Director Lin Wojiang resigns from his concurrent position as secretary-general, and Yao Xijiu is appointed as the Association's secretary-general. 4. The Association will add the position of chairman of the board, with Director Wang Xiaolai appointed as the Association's chairman. 5. Chairman Jiang is appointed as honorary chairman of the board. 6. Secretary-General Yao is requested to make efforts to develop all matters within the Association. In January of the 24th year of the Republic of China, the board of directors further resolved the following matters: 1. Chen Qingyun, Shen Deshe, Zeng Yijing, Li Jingcong, Nie Kaiyi, Li Ruyan, Wu Renshuo, and Yao Xijiu are added as directors of the Association. 2. Managing Director Lin Wojiang resigns, so Director Huang Bingheng is elected as managing director. Yu Zhaolin is also re-appointed as a director of the Association. 3. Managing Director Shi Liangcai passed away, so Director Zhang Huichang is re-elected as managing director, and Li Dachao is re-appointed as a director of the Association. The organization of the head office is now more complete than before, with one honorary chairman, one chairman, twenty-nine directors, seven managing directors, and one secretary-general, listed as follows:

Honorary Chairman: Jiang Zhongzheng; Chairman: Wang Xiaolai; Directors: Wang Xiaolai, Wang Zhengting, Wang Zhiyuan, Kong Xiangxi, Zhu Qinglan, Wu Renshuo, Wu Tiecheng, Du Yuesheng, Li Fusun, Li Jingcong, Li Dachao, Yu Zhaoqi, Shen Deshe, Lin Kanghou, Hu Wenhu, Hu Yunzhuang, Yao Xijiu, Chen Guangfu, Chen Qingyun, Zhang Huichang, Zhang Gongquan, Zhang Boling, Huang Bingheng, Zeng Yijing, Yu Qiaqing, Liu Peiquan, Li Ruyan, Nie Kaiyi, Dai Kuisheng; Managing Directors: Wang Xiaolai, Wang Zhengting, Kong Xiangxi, Wu Tiecheng, Lin Kanghou, Zhang Huichang, Huang Bingheng; Secretary-General: Yao Xijiu.

Establishing Branches in Provinces, Cities, and Overseas: In January of the 24th year of the Republic of China, the board of directors resolved to establish branches in provinces, cities, and overseas. The Association submitted a report to the Executive Yuan and sent letters to the provincial and municipal governments, inviting local organizations to organize. The Association then considered the situation and successively sent personnel to various provinces to plan and carry out the work. Branches were established in Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian, Hunan, Jiangsu, and Henan. The remaining provinces are in the process of selecting personnel to contact and prepare, in order to achieve the popularization of aviation patriotism throughout the country. Regarding overseas affairs, in April of last year, Chairman Wang Xiaolai, Managing Director Wang Zhengting, and Director and Secretary-General Yao Xijiu participated in a sightseeing tour to the Philippines and held preliminary consultations with local overseas Chinese, which have made considerable progress and are being planned.

Publishing Periodic Aviation Publications for the Public: In September of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, the board of directors resolved to publish "Aviation Books and Newspapers" once a month. Starting in September, it was changed to "Aviation Bi-Monthly," published twice a month. It has now been published for fourteen issues and has been praised by all sectors of society. Currently, there are subscribers in Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Henan, Anhui, Gan, Fujian, Hebei, Shandong, Hunan, Hubei, Guangdong, Guangxi, Yunnan, Guizhou, Chahar, Suiyuan, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Sichuan, Gansu, and other provinces, as well as overseas in Singapore, the Philippines, Japan, the United States, and other places. The reason why this publication has achieved today's success is due to the needs of the times and the enthusiastic support of compatriots from all over the world. In the future, we must strive to improve it, so that it can make greater contributions to aviation academia.

Establishing a Memorial Stele for Martyr Huang Yuquan: Martyr Huang Yuquan was a rising star in China's aviation world. During the January 28th Incident, he flew his plane to the front and died for his country at the Hongkou Airfield. In January of the 24th year of the Republic of China, at the fourth board meeting of the Association, Director Zhang Huichang proposed establishing a memorial stele for Martyr Huang to preserve his memory. It was resolved to proceed accordingly. The Aviation Committee was requested to designate the location of the stele next to the Xiao De Memorial Stele at the Hongqiao Airport in Shanghai. Donations were collected from the directors and entrusted to the China Stone Company for construction. Chairman Lin of the National Government was requested to inscribe the stele's inscription, Chairman Wang Xiaolai of the Association wrote the inscription on the stele, Director Zhang Huichang narrated the biography, and Directors Wu Tiecheng, Wang Zhengting, and Lin Kanghou and Chen Qingyun wrote inscriptions separately. The stele was unveiled at the Hongqiao Airport on October 1st of the 24th year of the Republic of China. More than a hundred people attended, including directors of the Association, captains of the solicitation teams, and representatives from various agencies and organizations. Chairman and Mayor Wu reported on the preparation process, Chairman Wang reported on the life and deeds of Martyr Huang, and Mr. Yupei, the martyr's brother and current principal of the Central Aviation Luoyang Branch School, gave a reply. The entire venue was filled with an atmosphere of grief and solemnity.

Opening the China Flying Club: The nature of the Flying Club is to arouse the people's interest in aviation, connect the feelings of all sectors of the aviation community, study aviation-related academics, and lay the foundation for national primary aviation talent reserves. All countries have established such clubs, and they are large in scale. In the 23rd year of the Republic of China, the Association submitted a request to establish the "Shanghai Flying Club." The proposed charter seemed to focus on education. At the fourth board meeting in January of the 24th year of the Republic of China, five directors, Zhang Huichang, Nie Kaiyi, Wu Renshuo, Li Ruyan, and Yao Xijiu, were appointed to re-draft the plan, change the name to "China Flying Club," draft the charter and practical guidelines, and prepare a budget estimate. The Aviation Committee approved it for record. It was officially established on the Double Tenth Festival last year. Young people across the country competed to join as members, which was extremely enthusiastic. The current work is as follows: (1) Holding free sightseeing flights. In order to promote social atmosphere, advocate aviation interest, and get used to aerial movements, the club holds free sightseeing flights. Participants are not divided by gender, and those who are physically strong and good at flying are not charged, but a miscellaneous fee of two yuan is charged for transportation. It began on March 1st of this year. One session is held every Wednesday, Saturday, and Sunday, for a total of twelve flights. More than one hundred and seventy people have participated. City sightseeing flights are also held, and participation is also extremely enthusiastic. (2) Flight training class. In order to promote aviation interest and cultivate aviation technical talent, the club requested government approval to hold civil training matters and hold flight training classes, using the latest type of aircraft and the most complete curriculum, and hiring experienced aviation experts to serve as coaches. The registration period is from April 20th to the 15th of this month, and the number of participants is extremely crowded.

General Situation of Fundraising to Purchase Aircraft for Birthday Celebrations

This year in September, it happened to be Chairman Jiang's 50th birthday celebration. Chairman Jiang has never made a show of celebrating birthdays, but all sectors of our country, for this great leader of the industry, who has dedicated himself to the party and the country for decades, working hard and enduring hardships, seeking survival for the country, and seeking rejuvenation for the nation, cannot but have some celebration. In order to express our respect and admiration for Chairman Jiang's enthusiasm for working hard for the party and the country, the Association launched a fundraising campaign to purchase aircraft as a memorial for Chairman Jiang's 50th birthday, different from the extravagant and wasteful customs of the world, and to carry out a practical movement to save the country, promote aviation patriotism, and strengthen national defense. I think Chairman Jiang will be able to sympathize with this. Since its launch, all parties have responded enthusiastically, which shows how much he is loved. The progress of the situation is briefly described as follows:

Progress in Shanghai: At the 30th meeting of the Standing Committee of the Association, it was resolved to raise 1 million yuan in Shanghai to purchase 10 aircraft, named the Zhongzheng Squadron, to promote the campaign. Shanghai Mayor Wu invited leaders from all walks of life to the municipal government on March 10 to discuss the progress methods. It was decided that the fundraising period would be six months (from March to August). Fundraising methods: divided into ordinary and special types. Ordinary birthday gift donations can be donated by each person at will. Special donations use birthday gift coupons. The denominations of the gift coupons are divided into: Heaven-grade 10,000 yuan, Earth-grade 5,000 yuan, Middle-grade 1,000 yuan, Right-grade 800 yuan, Harmony-grade 600 yuan, Peace-grade 500 yuan, Fortune-grade 400 yuan, Prosperity-grade 300 yuan, Longevity-grade 200 yuan, and Happiness-grade 100 yuan. Wu Tiecheng, Wang Xiaolai, Yao Xijiu, Li Dachao, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Xingya, Cai Jingjun, Du Yuesheng, Qian Xinzhi, Zhang Xiaolin, Lu Bohong, Xu Jiying, Chen Guangfu, Lin Kanghou, Shao Yanshan, Yu Zuoting, Wang Yansong, Huang Zhaoxiong, Wu Kaixian, Jiang Huaishu, Zhu Xuefan, Zhou Xuexiang, Tong Xingbai, Yu Qiaqing, Mrs. Mei Huaquan, Mu Ouchu, Zhang Weiru, Xu Busun, Gu Xinyi, Wang Yiting, Zhang Shouyong, Li Zhaohuan, Weng Zhilong, etc. were appointed as committee members. Wu Tiecheng, Wang Xiaolai, Pan Gongzhan, Yu Zuoting, and Zhang Shouyong were appointed as standing committee members. Yao Xijiu was appointed as secretary-general, and Li Dachao was appointed as general manager. The office was located at the YMCA in Baxianqiao. On April 28, a second meeting was held to decide to publish an announcement in the newspaper inviting people from all walks of life to participate in the launch, so as to achieve significant results, and to discuss matters related to organization, publicity, promotion, and liaison. Regarding the clearing of donations, in order to order the aircraft, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Yao Xijiu, Li Dachao, etc. were appointed to handle it. Since this meeting, the office has started to solicit sponsors. Those who have replied to agree include: in addition to the committee members appointed at the first meeting, who are of course sponsors, there are leaders from various agencies, organizations, factories, companies, banks, schools, etc., Ye Zhuotang, Li Tingan, He Bingsong, Tang Shoumin, Chen Hong, Zhao Jinqing, Ma Deji, Chu Huiseng, Chen Taoyi, Fang Jiaobo, Song Ziliang, Li Fuhou, Guo Shun, Bei Songsun, Wang Xiaoying, Hu Xiyuan, etc. can also be seen to be enthusiastic participants.

Various Organizations Plan to Raise Funds: Various organizations are very enthusiastic about fundraising for aircraft purchases to commemorate the event. Those who have been contacted and decided include: various agencies under the municipal government plan to raise tens of thousands of yuan, the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association plans to raise 100,000 yuan, the Miscellaneous Grain Industry Association plans to raise 90,000 yuan to purchase an aircraft, named "Miscellaneous Grain," the Exchange plans to raise tens of thousands of yuan, the Municipal Education Association plans to raise 90,000 yuan, the General Labor Union plans to raise 20,000 yuan, the China Women's Relief Association for Northeast Compatriots will transfer the remaining 8,000 yuan to donate, and the Wheel Navigation Industry and Hardware Industry Associations will each subscribe to a Middle-grade special birthday gift coupon, totaling 2,000 yuan. The Party and National Flag Promotion General Bureau suggested organizing a Party and National Flag promotion and publicity group, so that the city will universally purchase Party and National Flags, and 15% of the sales price will be transferred to purchase aircraft for birthday celebrations. Shanghai Xianghu Company, from April to the end of August, will donate half of all sales of ink and Xianghu to the Association. Separate letters have been sent to introduce this to various agencies and organizations, which have done their best to support. Shanghai Candy Company plans to sell 50,000 yuan worth of exquisite candies, and half of the proceeds will be donated to this. These are the fundraising plans of various organizations.

Donations from Theater Performances and Amusement Parks: In order to raise funds widely and complete the mission on schedule, the Association sent letters to all entertainment venues and movie theaters in the city, requesting to set aside one day to donate all business income to purchase aircraft for birthday celebrations. Theaters have responded one after another, including the Enpaiya Grand Theater, the Golden Grand Theater, the Great World Amusement Park, the Common Stage Grand Theater, the Great Stage Grand Theater, and comedian Zhang Ye'er's performance at the Central Grand Theater. After receiving this chain, within 24 hours, 15 copies should be copied, one copy kept for oneself, and one national currency yuan attached to the aircraft purchase memorial meeting. The remaining 14 copies should be sent to relatives and friends. The people of the whole country responded one after another, with dozens of cases every day.
